 Increase EMI or Loan Term? Most experts recommend extending EMI instead of extending loan period

 Mudra Yojana To promote micro, small and medium industries (MSME), the Modi government has launched the Pradhan Mantri Mudra Yojana
 micro units deveopment and rifinance agency limited (mudra) naam kii is yojana ke tahat chote kaarobaariyon ko lone ke taur par sahyog diya jaataa he

 iske tahat aapako 50 hajaar rupee tak kaa lone diya jaataa he

 teesri shrenee he tarun

 Startup India: The Modi Government launched the Startup India scheme on January 16, 2016 to promote businessmen who are giving birth to innovation and new dimensions in the country 
 iske tahat desh main starpeps ko har tarah kaa sahyog muhaiyaa kiye jane kii koshish he

 Jan Aushadhi Kendra: Apart from providing loan facility to those who start their business, the government is also giving an opportunity to earn money by opening Jan Aushadhi Kendra
 sarkaar kii yojana he ki kasbon or shaharon main jan aushadhi centre khole jaaen

 aap chahen to jagah kiraaye par lekar bhi isaki shuruyaat kar sakate hai

 5 lakh rupee tak kaa sahyeg miltaa he
 This support will be given every month as 15% of your monthly earnings
 har maheene aapako adhiktam 10 hajaar rupee tak sahyog ke taur par die jaaenge

 unka kahana he ki sarkaar sarvocch nyaayalay ke aadesh kaa sanmaan karti he
 Under this, she will give license to those who will follow the law of the state government issued in this case
 jo aisa nahin karenge, un par karrwai hogi
 Earlier on Tuesday, the Supreme Court made it clear that she wants to see dance bars started in Maharashtra and that too within just two days
 sunwaayee ke dauraan adaalat ne kaha ki court mahilaon ko jeevanyaapan karne kaa mauka dena chahta he or sarkaar unke jeevanyaapan ke adhikaar ko chhinana chaahati he
 In such a situation, the government should abide by the constitutional responsibility
 isi ke saath supreme court ne kaha he ki jin baar karmchaariyon ke khilaaf aapraadhik maamle darj hai, unhen kaam par nahin rakhaa jayega
 Bar owners will give this assurance in writing
 dance baar maamle kii agali sunwaayee shuukravaar ko hogi
 Till that time, the Maharashtra government has to follow the court order and file the report
 tippaniyan Explain that while the Supreme Court has clearly said that the dance bar should start, all the political parties of Maharashtra are united against it
 yahi vajah he ki sarkaar kanoon ke sahare dance baar kii rokthaam par lagi he
 He finds this issue to be a hindrance in the law and order of the state
 rajya kii bijepi sarkaar ne isi ke chalate sarvadaleey samiti se manjuur masaude ke tahat dance baar chalaane ke liye niyam or shart rakhi he
 The state legislature has approved this draft as a law and sent it to the President for final approval
 isse pehle chaar dance baar maalikon ko mili license yah kah kar radd kar die gaye ki unhone kanoon kaa ulanghan kiya he
 To which the Supreme Court objected that government law and order is not suitable for running the dance bar
 isse pehle mangalvaar ko supreme court ne spasht kar diya kii vah maharashtra main dance baar shuru hue dekhnaa chaahati he or vah bhi sirf do dinon ke bheetar
 During the hearing, the court said that the court wants to give women a chance to live and the government wants to take away their right to live
 aise main sarkaar ko sanvaidhanik jimmedaari kaa paalan karnaa chahie
 With this, the Supreme Court has said that the employees against whom criminal cases are filed, will not be hired
